While Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) offers a promising direction for grounding LLMs in repository context, existing RAG pipelines rely on static retrieval and lack the reasoning needed to identify faulty code accurately. In this work, we present BLAgent, a novel agentic RAG framework for file-level bug localization that integrates three key ideas: (i) code structure-aware repository encoding with path-augmented AST-based chunking, (ii) dual-perspective query transformation capturing both structural and behavioral signals, and (iii) two-phase agentic reranking combining symbolic inspection with evidence-grounded reasoning. Unlike prior graph-based or multi-hop agentic approaches, BLAgent performs bounded reasoning over a compact candidate set, balancing accuracy and cost. On SWE-bench Lite, BLAgent attains over 78% Top-1 accuracy with open-source models and over 86% with a closed-source model, while being over 18x cheaper than the strongest baseline using the same model. Ambiguous or weakly evidenced cases resolve fail-closed, while packetized state and event traces preserve an audit path.
  We examine one bounded reference implementation and ask what the released evidence can support about auditable, verify-gated completion. In the released verify-completed slice, the known-outcome invoked-event verify success share was 1,791/1,800 = 99.5%. This is an accounting measure over invoked verification events, not a task-completion, production-reliability, or benchmark-success rate. Task-level verify coverage is not computable; 1,762/1,801 rows came from one high-volume reporting cluster; and only 17 events were production-classified. A shadow Policy/Governance Verifier evaluation showed 1,526/1,548 = 98.58% rule agreement, 0/1,526 false-success among safe-to-proceed predictions, and blocked precision of 2/518 = 0.39%, so it remains advisory.
  The evidence supports a narrow conclusion: under observed conditions, a read-only verify gate plus packetized admission records made completion decisions inspectable and fail-closed. Claims about deployed operation, safety guarantees, outcome gains, task-level coverage, recovery effectiveness, or external validity remain outside scope.

Result: 在PrimeVul数据集上PairAcc达40.00%、F1-score达72.52%，PairAcc较最佳基线提升81.24%；在JITVUL数据集上PairAcc为28.67%；在542个冲突案例中正确解决了389个。

Conclusion: 多视角推理与协作验证对于实现鲁棒且全面的漏洞检测至关重要，辩论驱动的纠错机制能有效发现隐藏漏洞。

Abstract: Automated vulnerability detection is crucial for enhancing software security by identifying potential flaws that attackers could exploit, thereby reducing the reliance on labor-intensive manual code audits. Recent advancements have shifted towards leveraging large language models (LLMs) for vulnerability detection, with techniques like Vul-RAG and VulnSage demonstrating progress through structured prompting and external knowledge integration. However, these approaches typically rely on a single reasoning paradigm, limiting their ability to address the complex and diverse nature of real-world vulnerabilities. To overcome these limitations, we propose ReasonVul, a novel multi-perspective reasoning framework that harnesses cognitive synergy among three specialized LLM agents, each embodying a distinct reasoning mode. The framework begins with independent analyses of the source code, followed by a structured debate mechanism to resolve conflicts through iterative rebuttal and revision, ultimately converging on a collaborative judgment. Evaluated on the PrimeVul dataset, ReasonVul achieves a PairAcc of 40.00% and an F1-score of 72.52%, surpassing the best baseline by 81.24% in PairAcc. Further tests on the JITVUL dataset confirm its generalizability, with a PairAcc of 28.67%. Additionally, we analyzed 542 conflict cases and found that 389 were correctly resolved, highlighting the framework's ability to uncover hidden vulnerabilities through the error-correction mechanism driven by the debate. This work emphasizes the importance of multi-perspective reasoning and collaborative validation in achieving robust and comprehensive vulnerability detection in real-world software systems.

</details>


### [119] [Same Signal, Different Semantics: A Cross-Framework Behavioral Analysis of Software Engineering Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18332)
*Wei Ma,Zhi Chen,Jingxu Gu,Tianling Li,Shangqing Liu,Lingxiao Jiang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 通过对126种智能体配置（涵盖43个框架、64,380次SWE-bench运行）的大规模分析，发现相同的行为信号在不同框架下可能具有完全相反的效能含义。框架对行为差异的解释力（64%）远超LLM（10%），许多传统度量（如错误率）在不同配置中方向性相反，因此单一框架得出的行为规律不具备跨框架通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的软件工程智能体研究从单一框架中提取行为规则（如测试步骤应在代码修改之后、错误级联应短、轨迹应紧凑等），但这些规则是否跨不同智能体设计迁移（包括符号和幅度）尚未得到直接检验。

Method: 在生态系统规模上进行研究：收集来自43个框架、126种智能体配置的64,380次SWE-bench运行数据。通过固定LLM层或框架层分别分离框架效应和LLM效应，测量每种配置的行为-结果效应，并考察这些效应之间的一致性。

Result: 交换框架而保持LLM固定会产生巨大的行为差异。大多数信号上，不同配置不仅在效应幅度上不一致，在方向上也不一致。以错误率为例：47种配置在错误率较低时解决更多问题，而48种配置在错误率较高时解决更多。框架身份（64%）对配置间方差的解释力远大于LLM家族（10%）。

Conclusion: 相同的可观测行为信号在不同智能体配置中可能具有相反的含义。因此，任何单一框架得出的行为发现都需要跨配置验证后才能声称具有通用性。

Abstract: Behavioral studies of LLM-based software engineering agents extract operational rules about which trajectory shapes correlate with higher resolution rates: that a test step follows a code modification, that error cascades are short, or that trajectories are compact. Each rule is typically derived from a single framework, and whether it transfers, in sign as well as magnitude, to structurally different agent designs has not been directly tested.
  We address this at ecosystem scale: 64,380 SWE-bench runs from 126 agent configurations spanning 43 frameworks, where each configuration pairs an LLM with a framework (e.g., SWE-Agent, OpenHands) that supplies its tools and workflow. We separate framework effects from LLM effects by holding each layer fixed in turn, then measure one behavior-outcome effect per configuration and examine how those effects agree or disagree.
  Swapping the framework while the LLM is held fixed produces large behavioral differences in every action feature. On most signals, configurations disagree not merely in magnitude but in direction. Error rate is the cleanest case: 47 configurations resolve more issues when their error rate is lower, while 48 resolve more when it is higher. Five other continuous features and three of seven binary patterns from prior SE literature show similar directional disagreement. Framework identity accounts for more of this variation than LLM family: for mean turns, framework explains 64% of the between-configuration variance against the LLM's 10%.
  The implication is that the same observable behavioral signal can carry opposite meaning for different agent configurations. Behavioral findings from any single framework therefore warrant cross-configuration validation before being claimed as general.

</details>

### [120] [Detecting Verbatim LLM Copy-Paste in Homework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16336)
*Aizierjiang Aiersilan*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出SteganoPrompt，一种输入侧水印工具，通过在作业提示中嵌入不可见指令，让LLM在回复中自动生成签名，从而检测学生直接复制粘贴AI生成内容的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI文本检测方法（事后检测器、输出侧水印）存在不可靠、歧视非母语写作者、需要模型提供商配合等问题。教育者需要一种自己可直接控制的方法，来检测学生将作业提示直接粘贴给AI并提交原始回复的作弊行为。

Method: 开发SteganoPrompt工具，利用Unicode Tags区块（U+E0000–U+E007F）将任意可打印ASCII载荷编码为视觉不可见的指令，嵌入到作业提示中。LLM读取提示时会执行该隐藏指令，在回复中写入特定签名，从而暴露复制粘贴行为。

Result: 该工具为单页零依赖Web应用，编码后的字符串视觉上与原文本一致，能通过Word、Google Docs、PDF、Markdown、Slack、邮件及主流学习管理系统等常见复制粘贴渠道，且可被前沿模型可靠地分词处理。在7个LLM家族及代表性教育内容渠道上评估了合规性。

Conclusion: SteganoPrompt提供了一种教育者可独立控制的、针对特定作弊路径（直接复制粘贴AI输出）的检测方案，避免了现有方法的缺陷，以MIT许可证开源发布。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have made fluent essay writing, code drafting, and quiz answering instantly available to students at every level, from secondary school through graduate study. Many educators do not object to LLM use \emph{per~se}; what they need to detect is the case in which a student pastes the assignment prompt into a chatbot and submits the model's reply verbatim, without engaging with the work. Existing post-hoc AI-text detectors remain unreliable and have been shown to penalise non-native English writers, while output-side watermarks require cooperation from the model provider. We propose an alternative that the educator controls directly: an input-side watermark in which an invisible instruction is embedded inside the visible assignment prompt itself. An LLM that ingests the prompt verbatim quietly reads the hidden instruction and writes a tell-tale signature into its reply, exposing the copy-and-paste pathway specifically. We describe SteganoPrompt, a single-page, zero-dependency web tool that encodes an arbitrary printable-ASCII payload into the deprecated Unicode Tags block (\texttt{U+E0000}--\texttt{U+E007F}). The encoded string is visually identical to the original, survives common copy-paste channels (Word, Google Docs, PDF, Markdown, Slack, e-mail, the major learning-management systems), and is reliably tokenized by frontier models. We evaluate compliance across seven LLM families and a representative set of educational content channels. The work is informed by my experience as a graduate teaching assistant for an undergraduate software engineering course at the George Washington University. The tool is released under the MIT licence at \url{https://ezharjan.github.io/SteganoPrompt/}.

</details>


### [121] [Asking Back: Interaction-Layer Antidistillation Watermarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16462)
*Guang Yang,Amir Ghasemian,Fengchen Liu,Zhong Wang,Ninareh Mehrabi,Homa Hosseinmardi*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种交互层反蒸馏水印技术，通过在教师LLM的系统提示中嵌入行为标记（如追问、低频变体、陈述性重述），使攻击者在知识蒸馏时无意中继承这些行为特征，然后通过黑盒查询和LLM裁判进行检测。实验表明该方法在多种蒸馏模型和攻击场景下具有有效性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的针对LLM API的知识蒸馏防御方法（如token级水印、加密方案等）容易被改写攻击（如DIPPER paraphrasing）绕过，因为防御者无法控制攻击者的训练流程和logits。需要一种更高层次的、不受token改写影响的防御机制。

Method: 在教师模型部署时包装系统提示，间歇性诱导产生三种行为标记：显式追问、低频词汇变体、陈述性重述。被蒸馏的学生模型会在无意识中继承这些行为模式。防御方通过黑盒查询，使用人类验证的LLM裁判（Cohen's kappa = 0.84/0.78）来审计是否存在水印行为。

Result: 在Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct教师模型上对63个LoRA蒸馏学生模型进行了35,343次样本判断。行为水印的传递保真度：Gemma 88.9%、OLMo 80.9%、Qwen 45.2%。在非自适应DIPPER改写下，鲁棒性分解为教师自身上限约66.4%和学生相对保留率21-112%。低密度显式和隐式陈述性变体在基线以上传递。N=20实验室研究显示所有标记变体在0.22 Likert步长内。

Conclusion: 交互层是一个可行的反蒸馏水印设计空间，与token层、模型层和推理迹层防御互补。

Abstract: Detecting unauthorized knowledge distillation from a deployed LLM API is hard because the defender controls neither the attacker's training pipeline nor the next-token logits. Existing defenses operate on the teacher's output tokens -- biasing the next-token distribution (green-list watermarks, cryptographic schemes, antidistillation sampling) or rewriting outputs after generation. Recent work shows a paraphrasing attacker can strip these signals without losing the underlying knowledge.
  We propose interaction-layer antidistillation watermarks, which move the trace one layer higher, into the teacher's interaction behavior: the defender wraps the teacher with a system prompt that intermittently induces a behavioral marker -- an explicit follow-up question, a low-frequency variant, or a declarative restatement. An oblivious distiller inherits the behavior, and the defender audits via black-box queries with a human-validated LLM-as-judge (Cohen's kappa = 0.84/0.78 on strong/style rubrics).
  Across 63 LoRA-distilled students under a Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct teacher (35,343 judged samples), behavioral watermarks transfer at 88.9% (Gemma) / 80.9% (OLMo) / 45.2% (Qwen) relative fidelity (H1, H2). Under non-adaptive DIPPER paraphrasing, robustness decomposes into a teacher-self ceiling (about 66.4%) and student-relative retention of 21-112%, with OLMo preserving the watermark above the teacher itself (H3, F-Amp). Low-density (about 20%) explicit and implicit declarative variants transfer above per-family baseline (H4, F-Style). An N=20 in-lab study (pre-registered Latin-square) shows all marker variants within 0.22 Likert step of baseline; TOST, Friedman, and Bonferroni-Wilcoxon support H5. The interaction layer is a viable design locus for antidistillation watermarking, complementary to token-, model-, and reasoning-trace-layer defenses.

</details>


### [122] [From AI-Generated Content to Agentic Action: Security and Safety Threats in Generative AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16471)
*Zelin Zhang,Qi Li,Jie Cao,Lingshuang Liu,Jianbing Ni*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文分析了生成式AI系统从内容生成扩展到数据检索、工具调用和动作执行后，在内容层、模型层和智能体层面面临的安全威胁，并指出现有防御机制依赖的制度协调远落后于能力部署速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI正从单纯的内容产出转向通过工具链和外部API执行实际操作的智能体系统，这一转变带来了新型安全威胁，但现有研究缺乏系统性的威胁分析和防御评估。

Method: 从攻击者访问需求、系统自主性和潜在危害范围三个维度，系统分析了内容层、模型层和智能体层三类威胁，并评估了检测、水印、对齐和智能体防护等技术手段的适用性。

Result: 发现随着系统从生成内容转向执行实际操作，能力部署和攻击面扩展的速度持续快于防御响应，且多项防御机制依赖的制度协调机制在当前治理安排中尚不存在。

Conclusion: 生成式AI向智能体系统的演变带来了更严峻的安全挑战，现有治理框架不足以支撑必要的制度协调，安全防护亟需追赶系统能力的扩张速度。

Abstract: Generative AI systems are increasingly used not only to produce content but also to retrieve data, invoke tools, and execute actions. This work examines the security and safety implications of that shift across content-level, model-level, and agentic threats. We analyze how attacker access requirements, system autonomy, and the scope of potential harm change as models move from generating artifacts to executing operations through tool chains and external APIs. We then assess technical countermeasures including detection, watermarking, alignment, and emerging agentic safeguards, and show that several depend on forms of institutional coordination that current governance arrangements do not yet provide. Across the cases examined, capability deployment and attack-surface expansion repeatedly outpace defensive responses as systems move from generating content to executing real-world actions.

</details>


### [123] [Post-Quantum Discovery as a Governance Capability: Evidence-Based Cryptographic Visibility and Exposure Prioritisation in a Critical Service Provider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16549)
*Jelena Zelenovic,Leila Taghizadeh,Edoardo Pena-Gonzalez,Jaime Gomez Garcia,Bart Preneel*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文通过欧洲关键服务提供商的匿名案例研究，提出PQC准备应从“发现优先”策略开始，利用工具支持的密码资产盘点建立证据基线，并将密码发现视为一种治理能力，以将不确定性转化为可衡量的责任，支持基于风险的决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PQC准备的瓶颈不在于算法可用性，而在于密码可见性、依赖复杂性和分散的治理结构，亟需一种系统化的发现与治理方法。

Method: 采用匿名案例研究方法，对大型欧洲关键服务提供商的PQC准备过程进行深入分析，包括工具支持的密码资产盘点、暴露登记册的建立，以及基于资产关键性、机密寿命和迁移可行性的优先级排序。

Result: 发现阶段揭示了密码所有权分散、新旧环境证据质量不一、高度依赖第三方密码路线图等系统性挑战；引入暴露登记册有效支持了风险优先级排序。

Conclusion: PQC发现应作为一种治理能力来理解，它能够稳定组织知识，将密码不确定性转化为可衡量的问责机制，支持风险决策和生态系统协调，为面临“先收割后解密”威胁模型的组织提供可行经验。

Abstract: Post Quantum Cryptography (PQC) readiness is increasingly constrained not by algorithm availability, but by cryptographic visibility, dependency complexity, and fragmented governance. This paper presents an anonymised case study of a large European critical service provider that initiated PQC readiness through a discovery first strategy, utilizing tool supported cryptographic inventorying to establish an evidence based baseline prior to migration planning. The discovery phase revealed systemic challenges, including distributed cryptographic ownership, uneven evidence quality across legacy and modern environments, and high dependency on third party cryptographic roadmaps. To operationalise these findings, the organisation introduced a structured exposure register that enabled prioritisation based on asset criticality, confidentiality longevity, and migration feasibility. We argue that PQC discovery should be understood as a governance capability that stabilises organisational knowledge and converts cryptographic uncertainty into measurable accountability, supporting risk based decision making and ecosystem coordination. The results contribute actionable lessons for institutions pursuing crypto-agility and resilience under post quantum harvest now, decrypt later threat models.

</details>


### [124] [A Method for Securely Transmitting Large Video Files Using Chaotic Compression and Encryption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16563)
*Shiladitya Bhattacharjee,Subha Bhattacharya,Arnab Chatterjee,Sulabh Bansal,Saurabh Shukla*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出了一种结合混沌映射加密与霍夫曼无损压缩的同步数据压缩加密系统（SDCE），专为大视频文件设计，在降低计算开销的同时增强了数据安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统压缩与加密技术耗时且资源密集，不适用于实时应用，现有文献未能提出合适的联合策略。

Method: 将混沌映射（Logistic map）生成的伪随机序列用于XOR加密，并与霍夫曼无损编码集成在一个统一框架中，实现同步压缩与加密。

Result: 相比现有方法，该系统生成了更高的熵值和雪崩效应，提升了吞吐量、压缩比、峰值信噪比（PSNR），降低了比特率（BPC）和数据丢失率。

Conclusion: 该SDCE系统在增强数据隐私和完整性方面优于其他现有策略，适用于大视频文件的实时应用。

Abstract: Conventional techniques for compression and encryption are frequently laborious and resource-intensive, rendering them inappropriate for real-time applications. A plethora of research has been presented in the current literature to address these difficulties together; yet, it fails to propose any suitable strategy. Therefore, this study introduces an innovative simultaneous data compression and encryption (SDCE) system specifically designed for large video files. The methodology amalgamates chaotic map-based encryption with Huffman encoding for lossless compression into a cohesive framework, markedly diminishing computational overhead and processing duration while augmenting data security. The logistic map is utilized to produce a pseudo-random chaotic sequence for XOR-based encryption, guaranteeing robust security against unwanted access. The research findings demonstrate its efficacy in enhancing data privacy compared to other existing and related strategies, particularly in terms of generating greater entropy and avalanche effects. It produces superior throughput, compression ratio, peak signal-to-noise ratio (PSNR), and reduced bits per rate (BPC), along with a smaller percentage of data loss, which further supports its ability to provide enhanced data integrity compared to other existing methods.

</details>


### [125] [Stop Starving or Stuffing Me: Boosting Firmware Fuzzing Efficiency with On-demand Input Delivery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16798)
*Shandian Shen,Wei Zhou,Keming Zhao,Peng Liu,Chung Hwan Kim,Le Guan*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 针对固件模糊测试中异步输入投递的时序与数量问题，提出FIDO方法，通过静态与动态分析将输入处理流程分为三个阶段，在可用性检查点精准投递数据，并优化多路径调度。相比Fuzzware、MULTIFUZZ和SEmu，覆盖率提升最高115%，发现5个新漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有固件模糊测试直接套用通用软件的输入投递方式，未考虑固件输入异步、不确定的特性，导致"过载"（stuffing）或"饥饿"（starving）问题，严重削弱模糊测试能力。

Method: 利用固件必须在使用数据前检查输入可用性的特性，通过静态与动态分析将每个输入处理路径映射为三个阶段：输入检索、可用性检查、处理。在检查点按预期长度范围精确投递，并优化多输入路径的调度算法。

Result: FIDO作为插件集成到现有固件模糊测试工具中，相比Fuzzware和MULTIFUZZ的中位数代码覆盖率分别提升最高115%和54%，比需人工指定投递点的SEmu也提升最高19%，并显著加快已知漏洞发现速度，且发现5个新漏洞。

Conclusion: 通过语义感知的精确输入投递，FIDO有效解决了固件模糊测试中输入时机与数量的核心问题，验证了方法有效性，发现了真实世界的新漏洞。

Abstract: Firmware fuzzing has gained attention for identifying firmware bugs. However, current approaches often directly integrate fuzzing tools for general software. General software receives input as it encounters I/O functions, but firmware input can be received asynchronously and independently of the firmware's execution, with uncertain timing and quantity. Without full awareness of firmware's exceptions, existing solutions often imprudently deliver fuzzer-generated input to the firmware in an ad-hoc way. This either overwhelms the processing function of the firmware (stuffing) or fails to deliver enough input data to trigger input processing functions (starving). In both cases, fuzzing capability is weakened.
  In this paper, we comprehensively investigate the input delivery issue. To determine the optimal timing and quantity for delivering test cases, we leverage the fact that firmware has to check input availability before using data. So we employ static and dynamic analysis to map each input processing route into three stages: input retrieval, availability check, and processing. This recovered semantic information allows the fuzzer to accurately deliver input at the availability check points within the expected length range. For multiple input routes problem, we also optimize the scheduling algorithm to reach more diverse routes. Our prototype, named FIDO, can serve as an add-on to existing firmware fuzzers to enhance their test-case delivery effectiveness. Compared to ad-hoc input delivery methods used in Fuzzware and MULTIFUZZ, FIDO increases their median code coverage by up to 115% and 54%, respectively. Compared to SEmu, which requires humans to manually specify input delivery points, FIDO still improves its coverage by up to 19%. As a result, FIDO discovers known bugs significantly faster and also identifies five previously unknown bugs.

</details>


### [126] [Universal Graph Backdoor Defense: A Feature-based Homophily Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16815)
*Mengting Pan,Fan Li,Chen Chen,Xiaoyang Wang*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于节点局部特征一致性的通用图后门防御框架，通过邻居感知重构损失检测后门节点，并结合鲁棒训练策略消除触发器影响，有效防御了基于子图和基于特征的两种图后门攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图后门防御方法主要针对子图后门攻击，依赖"中毒目标节点与子图触发器显式连接"的假设，无法有效防御新兴的基于特征的后门攻击。因此需要研究一种通用的图后门防御方法。

Method: 1. 从特征同质性角度研究两种攻击类型的共同影响；2. 利用节点级局部特征一致性（通过邻居感知重构损失建模）区分后门节点与干净节点；3. 开发鲁棒训练策略消除触发器影响并降低检测不确定性带来的噪声。

Result: 大量实验表明，该框架能显著降低攻击成功率，并在基于子图和基于特征的攻击下保持有竞争力的干净准确率。

Conclusion: 无论触发器机制如何，图后门攻击诱导的后门节点比干净节点表现出更低的基于特征的同质性（局部特征相似性存在差异），利用这一差异可有效实现通用图后门防御。

Abstract: Graph neural networks (GNNs) have achieved remarkable success in relational learning. However, their vulnerability to graph backdoor attacks (GBAs) poses a significant barrier to broader adoption in high-stakes applications. Despite recent advances in graph backdoor defense (GBD), existing methods primarily focus on subgraph-based GBAs, relying on the assumption that poisoned target nodes are explicitly connected to subgraph triggers. Our empirical results reveal that such structure-centric approaches fail to defend against emerging feature-based GBAs that preserve graph topology. Therefore, in this paper, we study a novel problem of universal graph backdoor defense. First, we investigate the shared effects of both attack types from a feature-based homophily perspective, which characterizes local feature consistency between nodes and their neighborhoods. Thorough theoretical and empirical analyses demonstrate that, regardless of trigger mechanisms, backdoors induced by GBAs exhibit lower feature-based homophily than clean nodes, indicating a discrepancy in local feature similarity. Motivated by this insight, we propose to leverage node-level local feature consistency, modeled by a neighbor-aware reconstruction loss, to distinguish backdoors from clean nodes. Then, a robust training strategy is developed to eliminate trigger effects while reducing noise induced by detection uncertainty. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our framework significantly degrades the attack success rate and maintains competitive clean accuracy under both subgraph-based and feature-based attacks.

</details>

Abstract: This study proposes a lightweight Zero-Knowledge authentication model supported by QR codes. The approach is based on the Schnorr authentication protocol and provides an additional security layer against replay attacks through nonce and timestamp mechanisms. The proof data generated by the prover is embedded within a QR code and transmitted to the verifier. Thus, the system enables verification of knowledge of the secret key without revealing it. ### [128] [Securing LLM Agents Need Intent-to-Execution Integrity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16976)
*Wenjie Qu,Ming Xu,Peiran Wang,Shengfang Zhai,Jiaheng Zhang,Dawn Song*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文论证了保护LLM智能体安全需要首先定义端到端的正确性属性，提出了"意图到执行完整性"概念，并推导出四个必须同时满足的完整性属性：工具完整性、指令完整性、判断完整性和数据流完整性。通过分析现有防御机制，发现它们仅提供部分且不可组合的覆盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体安全研究缺乏一个充分的正确定义来描述"安全"意味着什么，也缺乏评估现有防御覆盖范围的原理性方法。随着第三方技能生态系统和直接用户环境访问的出现，传统假设工具可信的防御机制已经失效。

Method: 通过将LLM智能体与编译器进行结构类比，识别出两个根本问题来源（不可信数据摄入和不可信工具执行），并推导出四个必须同时满足的完整性属性，将其整合为"意图到执行完整性"。

Result: 现有智能体防御机制仅提供部分且不可组合的覆盖，在保护现代LLM智能体方面存在根本性漏洞。

Conclusion: 保护LLM智能体安全需要从定义端到端的正确性属性出发，本文提出的"意图到执行完整性"框架为评估和设计防御机制提供了理论基础。

Abstract: This position paper argues that securing LLM agents requires first defining an end-to-end correctness property that specifies when an agent's execution faithfully reflects the user's intent. Modern LLM agents operate over an \emph{intent-to-execution pipeline}, where natural-language instructions are translated into concrete system operations such as tool calls, API requests, and code execution. While recent defenses have made progress in constraining how agents construct tool calls, most existing formulations implicitly assume that tools are trusted. The emergence of systems such as OpenClaw, with open ecosystems of third-party skills and direct access to user environments, breaks this assumption and exposes new failure modes, including malicious or over-privileged components in the execution pipeline.
  Despite rapid progress in defense mechanisms, there is no adequate correctness property that defines what ``secure'' means for LLM agents, nor a principled way to evaluate the coverage of existing defenses. We observe that LLM agents are structurally analogous to compilers, where security violations correspond to mis-executions that do not preserve user intent. Drawing on this analogy, we identify two fundamental problem sources -- untrusted data ingestion and untrusted tool execution -- and derive four integrity properties that must hold simultaneously: \emph{Tool Integrity}, \emph{Instruction Integrity}, \emph{Judgment Integrity}, and \emph{Data Flow Integrity}. We call their conjunction \emph{intent-to-execution integrity}.
  Analyzing existing agentic defenses against these properties reveals that current systems provide only partial and non-compositional coverage, leaving fundamental gaps in securing modern LLM agents.

### [129] [The Range Shrinks, the Threat Remains: Re-evaluating LLM Package Hallucinations on the 2026 Frontier-Model Cohort](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17062)
*Aleksandr Churilov*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 对Spracklen等人关于代码生成LLM产生伪造包名（slopsquatting攻击面）的研究进行了复制，评估了2025-2026年五个前沿模型，发现幻觉率在4.62%-6.10%之间，模型间差异大幅缩小但威胁未消除，并发现了127个所有模型共有的伪造包名及若干新发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证Spracklen等人（USENIX Security '25）关于代码LLM产生伪造包名造成slopsquatting攻击面的发现是否在更新的模型中仍然成立，并进一步揭示跨模型共有的攻击面。

Method: 复制Spracklen的方法论，在2025年10月至2026年3月间发布的五个前沿代码LLM（Claude Sonnet 4.6、Claude Haiku 4.5、GPT-5.4-mini、Gemini 2.5 Pro、DeepSeek V3.2）上进行199,845对Python和JavaScript提示实验，将生成的包名与PyPI和npm主列表进行比对。

Abstract: Spracklen et al. (USENIX Security '25) showed that code-generating large language models hallucinate package names that do not exist on PyPI or npm at rates ranging from 5.2% on commercial models to 21.7% on open-source models, creating an attack surface for slopsquatting -- the registration of malicious packages under hallucinated names. We replicate their methodology on five frontier code-capable LLMs released between October 2025 and March 2026: Claude Sonnet 4.6, Claude Haiku 4.5, GPT-5.4-mini, Gemini 2.5 Pro, and DeepSeek V3.2. Across 199,845 paired Python and JavaScript prompts validated against PyPI and npm master lists, we measure overall hallucination rates between 4.62% (Claude Haiku 4.5) and 6.10% (GPT-5.4-mini) -- an order-of-magnitude compression of the inter-model spread observed by Spracklen, but not a retirement of the threat. Beyond replication, we identify a set of 127 package names (109 on PyPI, 18 on npm) that all five evaluated models invent identically, constituting a model-agnostic supply-chain attack surface that no single-model study can reveal. We further document a Python-over-JavaScript hallucination asymmetry that inverts Spracklen's 2024 finding, identify a Haiku-below-Sonnet inversion within the Anthropic family, and observe a Jaccard-similarity peak between DeepSeek V3.2 and GPT-5.4-mini (J = 0.343) suggestive of shared training-data origins.

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) cascade systems are designed to balance efficiency and performance by processing queries with lightweight models while selectively escalating complex cases to more powerful ones. However, the cascade design introduces new vulnerabilities through an expanded attack surface: the inclusion of lightweight front-end models and internal decision mechanisms introduces new weaknesses. In this work, we present the first study demonstrating that LLM cascade systems are susceptible to targeted adversarial manipulation, which disrupts both performance objectives and the intended cost advantages of the cascade design. We propose a novel attack framework that employs constrained sequential collaborative optimization of adversarial suffix under cascade dependencies, enabling simultaneous exploitation of lightweight models and decision mechanisms. This framework adapts to adversaries with varying capabilities, inducing controllable degradation in both cost-efficiency and accuracy. Unlike prior attacks targeting standalone models, our approach strategically leverages the cascade structure to achieve significantly stronger impact. Extensive experiments across diverse datasets and representative LLM cascade systems validate the practicality and severity of this attack. Our findings highlight the urgent need to rigorously scrutinize the security of LLM cascade systems and call for broader attention to the systemic risks inherent in such designs.

### [133] [ASPI: Seeking Ambiguity Clarification Amplifies Prompt Injection Vulnerability in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17324)
*Udari Madhushani Sehwag,Zhengyang Shan,Heming Liu,Dileepa Lakshan,Joseph Brandifino,Max Fenkell*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出ASPI基准测试，发现LLM智能体在澄清询问状态下比标准执行状态下更容易受到提示注入攻击，攻击成功率平均提升约20-30个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清询问行为被广泛认为是LLM智能体的理想特性，但其安全影响尚未被探索。研究者想探究从标准执行状态切换到澄清询问状态是否会增加智能体对提示注入攻击的敏感性。

Method: 构建了ASPI基准，包含728个任务-攻击场景，在匹配的执行设置和澄清设置下评估前沿LLM模型的脆弱性。执行设置中智能体在完全明确的指令上行动，澄清设置中智能体必须先请求并整合额外的用户输入。

Result: 在10个前沿LLM模型上的评估显示，澄清询问状态显著放大脆弱性。例如，o3的攻击成功率从1.8%上升到34.0%，Gemini-3-Flash从2.2%上升到35.7%。分解分析表明，这种差距源于状态相关的处理方式变化和智能体主动征求的澄清接口带来的通道特定效应。

Conclusion: 标准执行时安全评估系统性地低估了交互式智能体的攻击面，在完全指定任务下的鲁棒性并不能转化为在模糊任务下的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Clarification-seeking behavior is widely regarded as a desirable property of LLM agents, enabling them to resolve ambiguity before acting on underspecified tasks. However, the security implications of this interaction pattern remain unexplored. We investigate whether the transition from standard execution to a clarification-seeking state increases an agent's susceptibility to prompt injection attacks. We introduce ASPI (Ambiguous-State Prompt Injection), a benchmark of 728 task-attack scenarios that isolates clarification as a distinct agent state and measures how this state transition affects vulnerability under controlled conditions. Each benchmark instance is evaluated under matched execution and clarification settings: in the execution setting, the agent acts on a fully specified instruction and encounters adversarial content only through tool-returned data; in the clarification setting, the agent must first request and incorporate additional user input before acting. We evaluate ten frontier LLMs and find that clarification-seeking consistently and substantially amplifies vulnerability. For instance, attack success rises from 1.8% to 34.0% for o3 and from 2.2% to 35.7% for Gemini-3-Flash. A decomposition analysis reveals that this gap reflects both a state-dependent shift in how models process incoming content and a channel-specific effect arising from the agent-solicited clarification interface. These findings demonstrate that standard execution-time security evaluation systematically underestimates the attack surface of interactive agents, and that robustness under fully specified tasks does not translate to robustness under ambiguity. For reproducibility, our data and source code are available at https://github.com/scaleapi/aspi.

### [134] [LPG: Balancing Efficiency and Policy Reasoning in Latent Policy Guardrails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17329)
*Nanxi Li,Zhengyue Zhao,Chaowei Xiao*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出LPG（Latent Policy Guardrail）框架，通过将安全策略的内部推理解耦为连续潜变量，在保持低延迟和高可审计性的同时，实现了对动态安全策略的自适应判断。LPG-4B模型仅用10个潜变量token即可达到84.5%准确率和77.9% F1，速度比Qwen3-4B-Thinking快约11倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI安全护栏在面对动态定制的安全策略（不同用户、组织或监管场景）时，需要在推理能力（理解复杂策略上下文）与低延迟响应之间取得平衡，这是一个根本性的矛盾。

Method: LPG框架将策略意图解释和策略依据判断所需的内部推理解耦为连续潜状态（latent states），通过决策相关的语义信息进行监督学习。推理时仅输出紧凑的判决结果（锚定违规的政策条款），避免了显式推理带来的延迟。

Result: LPG-4B在政策护栏基准测试上达到84.5%平均安全准确率和77.9% F1（仅用10个潜变量token），性能超过最强的动态基线方法，同时在单样本评估设置下运行速度比Qwen3-4B-Thinking快约11倍。

Conclusion: LPG通过潜变量推理解耦的方式，有效解决了动态安全策略下推理能力与低延迟之间的冲突，为AI系统安全护栏的灵活部署提供了一种高效且可审计的新范式。

Abstract: Guardrails are a critical safety layer for modern AI systems, but their operating regime is changing. As LLMs are deployed as customized assistants, safety policies are increasingly specified at inference time by users, organizations, or regulatory contexts. This makes safety enforcement fundamentally dynamic: the guardrail should adapt to changing safety policies without retraining. Yet this requirement creates a fundamental tension: faithfully judging complex policy contexts demands reasoning capability, while practical deployment requires low-latency responses. We introduce Latent Policy Guardrail (LPG), a guardrail framework that learnssemantic latent deliberation over dynamic policies. LPG compresses the internal deliberation needed for intent interpretation and policy grounding into continuous states supervised by decision-relevant semantics. At inference time, it generates only a compact verdict anchored to the violated policy clauses, preserving auditability while avoiding the latency of explicit reasoning. Across policy guardrail benchmarks, LPG-4B reaches 84.5% average safety accuracy and 77.9% F1 by compressing deliberation into just 10 latent tokens, outperforming the strongest dynamic baseline while running roughly 11 times faster than Qwen3-4B-Thinking under the single-sample evaluation setup. Code and data are available at https://github.com/SaFo-Lab/Latent_Policy_Guard.

### [135] [Rethinking Side-Channel Analysis: Automated Discovery and Analysis of Side-Channel Leakage with LLM-Assisted Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17406)
*Zhen Xu,Zihao Wang,Yuhua Sun,XiaoFeng Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有侧信道分析主要依赖手动和碎片化方式，通常预设目标事件和已知信道，难以应对日益复杂的系统和应用。关键问题包括：哪些用户/系统事件是敏感的、如何系统化发现侧信道、如何在大规模分析中避免高昂的数据收集和模型训练成本。

Method: SCAgent采用三大技术：1) 基于LLM语义推理的智能体驱动系统探索，自动识别敏感目标；2) 对系统文档进行推理并结合显式验证，确保语义一致性、威胁模型可行性和信道可用性，缓解LLM幻觉风险；3) 基于基础模型的少样本学习范式，避免为每个信道-事件对训练专属模型；4) 引入对时间偏移鲁棒的特征提取层，弥合原始时序侧信道信号与表格型基础模型之间的差距。

Result: 在iOS平台上实例化SCAgent，针对非特权应用可观察的OS级侧信道进行评估。在标准基准（前台应用指纹识别、网站指纹识别）和新识别的流行应用内敏感活动检测任务中均取得有效结果。

Conclusion: SCAgent为侧信道风险分析提供了自动化、可扩展的解决方案，通过LLM驱动探索、文档推理验证和少样本学习，有效降低了人工成本和计算开销，未来可推广至更多平台和场景。

Abstract: Side-channel attacks exploit unintended information leakage from system behavior and continue to pose serious privacy risks in modern platforms. Despite extensive prior work, side-channel analysis remains largely manual and fragmented, typically assuming predefined target events and a fixed set of known channels. As systems and applications grow increasingly complex, several fundamental questions remain unanswered: which user or system events are sensitive in practice, how side channels associated with these events can be systematically discovered without exhaustive manual effort, and how their leakage can be analyzed at scale without prohibitive data collection and model training costs. To address these questions, we present SCAgent, an automated framework for side-channel risk analysis. To identify sensitive targets beyond manually specified events, SCAgent performs agent-driven system exploration guided by LLM-based semantic reasoning. To systematically discover side channels while mitigating the risk of LLM hallucination, it reasons over system documentation and incorporates explicit verification to enforce semantic consistency, threat-model feasibility, and per-channel usability. To enable scalable analysis under limited data, SCAgent adopts a few-shot learning paradigm based on foundation models, avoiding the need to train bespoke models for each channel--event pair. To bridge the gap between raw time-series side-channel signals and tabular foundation models, SCAgent further introduces a time-shift--robust feature extraction layer that enables effective downstream analysis. We instantiate SCAgent on iOS as a first step, focusing on OS-level side channels observable by unprivileged applications. Our evaluation spans standard benchmarks such as foreground app and website fingerprinting, as well as newly identified sensitive in-app activities in popular applications.

</details>


### [136] [Trust No Tool: Evaluating and Defending LLM Agents under Untrusted Tool Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17453)
*Lecheng Yan,Ruizhe Li,Xicheng Han,Wenxi Li,Binwu Wang,Longyue Wang,Chenyang Lyu,Guanhua Chen*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种新型的LLM agent安全威胁——认知中毒（cognitive poisoning），即恶意工具在探索阶段表现正常以积累信任，仅在特定隐藏状态满足时才产生危害。作者构建了TRUST-Bench基准数据集，提出非对称惩罚指标GuardedJoint和风险评分框架VISTA-Guard，实验表明该方法在域内和域外迁移评估中均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有agent安全研究默认工具反馈可信，忽略了恶意工具通过良性反馈积累信任后再实施攻击的风险。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究认知中毒这一新型失效模式。

Method: 构建TRUST-Bench基准（1,970个隐藏触发工具劫持样本）；提出GuardedJoint非对称惩罚指标；开发VISTA-Guard框架，通过将多步工具交互抽象为结构化环境变量编码信任形成动态，对最终可执行动作进行风险评分。

Result: 在GuardedJoint指标下，VISTA-Guard达到域内84.2、平衡域外迁移56.9的成绩，而只优化安全或效用单一方面的方法得分为零。

Conclusion: 在黑盒工具生态中，防御的关键目标不仅是局部提示文本或工具描述，而是整个交互轨迹中的信任形成方式以及最终动作中的信任承诺。

Abstract: Tool-using LLM agents increasingly rely on external tools to make consequential decisions, yet most existing agent-security benchmarks and defenses implicitly assume that tool feedback is trustworthy once a tool has been selected. We study a different failure mode, cognitive poisoning, in which a malicious tool behaves plausibly during exploration, accumulates trust through benign-looking feedback, and becomes harmful only when hidden state conditions align with the final executable action. To study this setting, we construct TRUST-Bench, a task-conditioned benchmark of 1,970 hidden-trigger tool-compromise episodes with matched safe controls, introduce an asymmetric penalty metric, GuardedJoint, to better reflect real deployment risk, and present VISTA-Guard, a backbone-agnostic framework for final-action risk scoring. The core idea is to abstract multi-step tool interaction into structured environment variables that encode trust-formation dynamics and then score the risk of the final executable action from this trajectory-conditioned representation. Experiments show that prompt-centric heuristics, scalarized features, and zero-shot judges fail in this regime, whereas trajectory-aware final-action scoring yields strong in-domain discrimination and remains effective under balanced out-of-distribution transfer. Under GuardedJoint, VISTA-Guard reaches $84.2$ in-domain and $56.9$ on balanced out-of-distribution evaluation, while methods that optimize only one side of the safety--utility tradeoff collapse to zero. These findings support a broader view of agent security in black-box tool ecosystems: the decisive defense target is not local prompt text or tool descriptors alone, but the way trust is formed across the interaction trajectory and committed through the final action.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Polynomial multiplication is fundamental in lattice-based cryptography. While the Number Theoretic Transform (NTT) enables fast multiplication, it imposes constraints on the modulus of the coefficient field. Hafiz et al. (2025) addressed this limitation by analyzing the incomplete NTT, which combines a truncated NTT with conventional multiplication methods In this work, we revisit Toom-4 multiplication in the context of incomplete NTT. Although Toom-4 is asymptotically faster than Karatsuba, its precise cost has not been expressed in a form compatible with the incomplete NTT framework. We present a concrete Toom-4 implementation and derive explicit operation counts that separate additions/subtractions and multiplications over the coefficient field. Our analysis based on addition chains yields a simple cost model for incomplete NTT. Using this model, we analyze hybrid strategies combining Toom-4, Karatsuba, and incomplete NTT. ### [138] [AI Agents May Always Fall for Prompt Injections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17634)
*Sahar Abdelnabi,Eugene Bagdasarian*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文指出当前AI智能体的主流防御范式（数据-指令分离）无法有效检测通过上下文操控发起的提示注入攻击，反而会损害上下文恰当行为。作者引入“情境完整性”（CI）理论重新阐释该问题，揭示了攻击的本质是违反情境规范的信息流动，并论证了防御的不可可能性：攻击者总能构造看似合法的上下文，而严格规范也会误伤合法流动。研究认为当前防御面正在缩小，并提出基于CI的评估框架与对齐方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示注入防御（数据-指令分离）存在根本性缺陷：既无法检测通过上下文操控的攻击，又会破坏AI智能体的情境恰当行为。需要新的理论框架来理解问题的本质。

Method: 将提示注入问题重新置于情境完整性（CI）理论框架下分析，识别出三种攻击类型（误表述流动、操控规范、混合多流动），并论证了防御的不可可能性。

Result: 揭示了当前防御范式只能应对未来攻击面中不断缩小的部分；证明攻击者总能找到使被阻断流动看似合法的新上下文。

Conclusion: 提示注入防御存在理论上的极限，需转向CI感知的对齐方法，才能应对前沿自主智能体面临的更复杂攻击。

Abstract: Prompt injection is the most critical vulnerability in deployed AI agents. Despite recent progress, we show that the prevailing defense paradigm (data-instruction separation) both fails to detect attacks that operate through contextual manipulation and degrades contextually appropriate behavior. We then recast prompt injection via the lens of Contextual Integrity (CI), a privacy theory that judges information flow compliance with contextual norms. This explains types of attacks that current defenses attempt to patch and predict advanced ones future agents will face. We develop unique benign and attack scenarios that force an agent to violate the norms by (1) misrepresenting the flow, (2) manipulating norms, or (3) mixing multiple flows. This reframing suggests an impossibility result: an adversary can always construct a context under which a blocked flow appears legitimate, or a defender who tightens norms will block genuinely legitimate flows. Our findings suggest that current research addresses a shrinking fraction of future attack surfaces. Instead, through CI, we offer a principled framework for evaluating context-sensitive failures, and designing CI-aware alignment for the frontier autonomous agents.

</details>

### [139] [GRASP: Graph Agentic Search over Propositions for Multi-hop Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16598)
*Stockton Jenkins,Ramya Korlakai Vinayak,Junjie Hu*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: GRASP是一种新型智能检索系统，通过依赖感知的查询分解和三层层次图结构（实体-命题-段落）实现多跳问答，在保持高准确率的同时大幅降低token消耗（比基线方法低30-50%），并提出了成功率经济（success economy）这一效率感知评估指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能检索系统结合知识图谱虽能提升多跳问答效果，但面临两大问题：索引时图谱构建成本高昂，以及推理时token消耗累积严重。亟需一种既能保持高准确率又能显著降低token使用量的方法。

Method: GRASP引入依赖感知的查询分解策略，将多跳查询拆解为可执行的子任务并动态调整子智能体数量；构建实体-命题-段落三层层次图，利用实体层进行精准遍历，命题层通过倒数排名投票实现高召回率段落检索。

Result: 在MuSiQue和2WikiMultihopQA的开放检索设定中，GRASP取得最高QA准确率，同时token使用量比IRCoT+HippoRAG2减少40-50%；在LongBench设定中，GRASP在三个数据集上EM和F1均领先，token使用量比次优方法少30%。

Conclusion: GRASP验证了效率感知评估的重要性，并倡导将token效率作为智能问答系统的标准评价维度，而不仅仅是追求准确率。

Abstract: Agentic retrieval improves multi-hop question answering by giving language models autonomy to iteratively gather evidence. Recent work augments these systems with knowledge graphs for structured traversal, but this combination introduces significant cost: expensive graph construction at index time and compounding token usage at inference time. We introduce Graph Agentic Search over Propositions (GRASP), an agentic system that simultaneously optimizes for high accuracy and minimal token usage in multi-hop question answering. Rather than executing a rigid, singular query, GRASP actively coordinates its retrieval strategy by decomposing multi-hop queries into dependency-aware plans. This enables GRASP to dynamically scale the number of sub-agents according to the complexity of the problem. Each sub-agent resolves its single-hop query by exploring a novel three-layer hierarchical graph of entities, propositions, and passages, using the entity layer for targeted traversal and the proposition layer for high-recall passage retrieval via reciprocal-rank voting. We evaluate GRASP on MuSiQue, 2WikiMultihopQA, and HotpotQA under two settings: open-corpus retrieval and extended context reasoning (LongBench). GRASP achieves the highest QA accuracy in the open retrieval setting on MuSiQue and 2Wiki while using 40-50 percent fewer tokens than IRCoT+HippoRAG2. Furthermore, GRASP leads on EM and F1 across all three datasets in the LongBench setting while using 30 percent fewer tokens than the next most accurate method. Finally, we introduce success economy - the amortized token cost per correct answer, weighted by difficulty - and advocate for efficiency-aware evaluation as a standard practice for agentic QA.

</details>


### [140] [Dynamic Deployment of Mobile Charging Trucks During Natural Disaster Evacuation: An Offline-to-Online Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16784)
*Rui Ma,Zilin Bian,Kaan Ozbay*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自适应风险感知的移动充电卡车部署框架（ARMD），用于在大规模疏散中动态部署移动充电卡车来补充固定充电站，通过离线预训练和在线自适应优化策略，在模拟飓风疏散环境中平均风险暴露降低高达71.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模疏散期间，电动汽车集中充电需求会导致固定充电站过载，造成长时间等待和风险暴露增加，现有方法难以应对这种动态不确定场景。

Method: 将移动充电卡车部署分解为风险感知资源分配（基于多智能体近端策略优化的分散部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程）和动态路径规划（时空旅行时间预测+滚动时域更新）两个子问题，采用离线预训练+在线自适应优化的范式。

Abstract: During large-scale evacuations, concentrated electric vehicle (EV) charging demand can overload fixed charging stations (FCSs), leading to prolonged waiting time and increased risk exposure. To address this challenge, this study proposes dynamically deploying mobile charging trucks (MCTs) to complement FCSs, and develops an Adaptive Risk-aware MCT Deployment (ARMD) framework for real-time operation. It divides the MCT deployment into two problems: risk-aware allocation of MCTs among FCSs and dynamic routing of MCTs to the assigned FCSs, and solves them under an offline-to-online paradigm. The resource allocation problem is formulated as a decentralized partially observable Markov decision process, and a multi-agent proximal policy optimization (MAPPO)-based policy is developed to coordinate multiple MCTs under decentralized observations. The policy is pre-trained offline in an evacuation simulator and adaptively refined online according to current evacuation context. For routing, a spatio-temporal travel time predictor is developed to support rolling-horizon route updates. The proposed framework is evaluated in a simulated hurricane evacuation environment built using real-world data from Hillsborough County, Florida. Experiments show that ARMD consistently outperforms offline optimization, online heuristic dispatch, and rolling-horizon optimization in reducing risk exposure. For demand perturbation scenarios, ARMD reduces average risk exposure by up to 71.1%, relative to the baseline without MCTs. In the case of fixed e-vehicle charging infrastructure or road link failures, ARMD achieves 39.3% to 60.5% reduction in average risk exposure, with its advantages becoming more pronounced as the severity of disruption increases. These results demonstrate the effectiveness and robustness of ARMD in enhancing mobile charging operations for realistic scenarios of uncertain evacuation conditions.

Abstract: Memory has become an increasingly important component of agentic systems, as these systems are expected to reason over long-term experience. Compared with unimodal settings, multimodal memory introduces additional challenges, including heterogeneous input integration, person-centric information alignment, and evidence aggregation across different granularities. ### [143] [Multi-LLM Systems Exhibit Robust Semantic Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17193)
*Weiyi Kong,Shiyang Lai,Jinghua Piao,James Evans*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 多LLM系统在封闭循环中会出现语义崩溃现象，即尽管词汇表面多样，但语义表征系统性趋同，且现有干预策略无法恢复语义多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从Lovelace到Turing关于机器能否创造新内容的辩论延续近两个世纪，多LLM系统在自主生成中的广泛应用使得这一经典问题得以通过实证方式重新检验。

Method: 对多LLM系统进行200至1000轮的封闭循环仿真，跨越多个模型家族，并测试12种干预策略（包括解码参数、提示设计、智能体组成、激活工程和强化学习），同时进行机制分析。

Result: 所有模型家族均表现出语义崩溃现象；12种干预策略均无法恢复语义多样性；机制分析表明语义崩溃并非由对齐或从众偏差导致，而是与自回归生成的内在属性一致。

Abstract: Whether machines can originate novel content has been debated for nearly two centuries, from Lovelace's assertion that no engine can "originate anything" to Turing's question of whether a machine can amplify ideas brought in from outside. Multi-large language model (LLM) systems, increasingly deployed for autonomous generation, reopen this question empirically. Here we show that such systems, operating in closed loops, exhibit semantic collapse: systematic convergence in semantic representations despite apparent lexical variation. Across model families, extended simulations of 200 to 1,000 rounds, the pattern remains consistent. Twelve intervention strategies, spanning decoding parameters, prompt design, agent composition, activation engineering, and reinforcement learning, fail to restore semantic diversity. Mechanistic analyses suggest that semantic collapse is not explained by alignment or conformity biases, but is consistent with intrinsic properties of autoregressive generation. Our results point to fundamental constraints in the ability of multi-LLM systems to sustain open-ended knowledge production in closed-loop settings.

### [144] [Human-Flow Digital Twin for Predicting the Effects of Mobility Introduction on Visitor Circulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17426)
*Chiharu Shima,Haruki Yonekura,Fukuharu Tanaka,Tatsuya Amano,Hirozumi Yamaguchi*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用人流数字孪生框架预测移动性引入措施效果的方法，通过多智能体模拟器训练访客决策模型，并在和歌山城公园的实际数据验证中取得了良好效果（空间人口分布余弦相似度超过0.7）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以准确预测引入移动性措施（如新增交通设施）后的人流变化，需要一种能够捕捉访客目的地选择行为并量化其影响的框架。

Method: 构建包含多智能体模拟器的人流数字孪生，利用干预前的人流数据、景点间距离、景点吸引力及出行量等特征训练每个智能体的决策模型（多层感知器），并通过改变距离或吸引力参数来模拟移动性引入效果。

Result: 在和歌山城公园的真实数据实验中，使用多层感知器决策模型复现移动性引入后的人流时，空间人口分布的余弦相似度超过0.7，验证了该方法能有效复现人流变化。

Conclusion: 该框架能有效预测移动性引入措施对人流量和流通模式的影响，为城市规划和交通管理提供可靠的决策支持工具。

Abstract: We propose a framework for predicting the effects of mobility introduction measures using a human-flow digital twin. This digital twin incorporates a multi-agent simulator that can represent how visitors choose destinations depending on factors such as their current location and the attractiveness of spots. We extract data on how visitors selected destinations with respect to measured pre-intervention human-flow data, inter-spot distances, spot attractiveness, and travel volumes, and use these data to train each agent's decision model of this simulator. The trained decision model is a function that takes a visitor's current state and surrounding environmental information as input and outputs which spot the visitor will move toward next. By expressing mobility introduction measures as changes to inter-point distances or to spot attractiveness, the framework can reproduce human flows with mobility introduction in the multi-agent simulator and thereby quantify effects such as changes in visitor counts and circulation. We evaluated the proposed method using human-flow data measured with and without introducing mobility within Wakayama Castle Park in Japan. When reproducing flows with mobility introduction using a multi-layer perceptron decision model, the cosine similarity of the spatial population distribution exceeded 0.7, confirming that the approach can replicate the flow changes caused by the mobility introduction.

</details>


### [145] [Reservation Based Smart Parking Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17650)
*Giacomo Cabri,Manuela Montangero,Filippo Muzzini,Roberto Wang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出一种双机制架构（动态缓冲区预约模块+星级声誉奖惩系统），通过SUMO仿真证明能有效减少“车位被占”问题，提升停车资源利用率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预约停车系统常出现用户到达时预留车位仍被前车占用（"No PARK"情况），导致系统可靠性下降，需要一种能动态适应并激励按时驶离的机制。

Method: 设计双机制架构：1) 预约模块采用动态大小的非可预约缓冲区来保障停车位可用性；2) 基于星级的声誉系统通过罚款和访问限制激励用户准时驶离，并在SUMO仿真器中验证。

Result: 仿真结果表明动态缓冲区策略在停车可用性与预约成功率之间取得了更好的平衡，有效减少了"NO PARK"实例，提高了资源利用率。

Conclusion: 该系统能逐步适应用户行为，缓解车位被占问题，提升城市宜居性，对智能城市和智能交通系统中的停车管理有实际价值。

Abstract: In the framework of Smart Cities and Intelligent Transportation Systems (ITS), efficient parking management is essential to reduce urban congestion and emissions. However, current reservation-based systems often encounter a scenario in which users find their reserved slot occupied by a previous occupant who failed to vacate on time ("No PARK" situation). This paper introduces a dual-mechanism architecture designed to enhance system reliability. A Reservation Module uses a dynamic size buffer of non-reservable slots to grant parking availability. A reputation-based Reward System exploits a "star-based" metric to incentivize punctual departures through financial penalties and access restrictions. The simulations conducted with the SUMO urban simulator are promising, showing that the dynamic buffer strategy provides a better tradeoff between parking availability and reservation success. By progressively adapting to users behavior, the proposed system mitigates "NO PARK" instances and improves resource utilization, significantly enhancing urban viability. Index Terms-Smart City, Intelligent transportation systems, Parking, Reservation systems, V2I, Reputation-based mechanisms, Smart Parking

</details>


### [146] [The Dynamics of Policy Gradient in Social Dilemmas with Partner Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18185)
*Benedict Russell,Chin-wing Leung,Paolo Turrini*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文通过解析方法研究带伙伴选择机制的策略梯度演化博弈，证明伙伴选择通过改变对手分布促进合作，并发现人口方差是合作产生的必要条件，同时建立了随机模型并推导出促进合作的充分条件及平稳分布的存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于伙伴选择促进合作的研究主要基于智能体仿真，缺乏解析解，本文旨在提供严格的理论分析。

Method: 对带伙伴选择的多智能体环境中的策略梯度动力学进行解析求解，利用二维维纳过程扩展动力学模型以捕捉随机效应，推导促进合作的充分条件和平稳分布的存在性。

Result: 证明伙伴选择改变对手分布和奖励景观从而促进合作；发现人口方差是合作产生的必要条件；推导出促进合作的充分条件；证明平稳分布的存在性；仿真验证随机模型准确捕捉策略梯度动力学，并阐明学习率对合作涌现的影响。

Conclusion: 伙伴选择机制能够通过改变对手分布来促进合作，人口方差是必要条件，所提出的随机模型能够有效刻画该动力学过程。

Abstract: In social dilemmas self-interested learning agents face the choice between the societal benefit of cooperation and the immediate reward of defection. Significant evidence exists on the benefits of assortment mechanisms such as partner selection for the emergence of cooperation, but this is largely available through agent-based simulations. In this paper, we provide an analytical solution to the problem, studying the policy-gradient dynamics in a multi-agent environment with partner selection. We show how partner selection changes the opponent distribution and hence the reward landscape, and prove this promotes cooperation under simple rules known from the literature. In particular, we find that population variance is a necessary condition for cooperation to emerge. Using a two-dimensional Wiener process, we extend the dynamics to capture the stochastic effects of partner selection and the resulting opponent distribution. We derive a sufficient condition for the population to be cooperation-promoting and prove the existence of a stationary distribution. Simulations confirm that the stochastic model accurately captures the policy-gradient dynamics and clarifies how the learning rate affects the emergence of cooperation.

</details>
